## God Nodes (most connected - your core abstractions)
1. `ProxyConfig` - 198 edges
2. `ContentRouter` - 190 edges
3. `CompressionStore` - 168 edges
4. `HeadroomProxy` - 140 edges
5. `ToolIntelligenceNetwork` - 130 edges
6. `create_app()` - 124 edges
7. `Memory` - 113 edges
8. `ok()` - 108 edges
9. `LocalBackend` - 107 edges
10. `TOINConfig` - 102 edges

## Surprising Connections (you probably didn't know these)
- `backend_config()` --calls--> `LocalBackendConfig`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_memory_system.py → headroom/memory/backends/local.py
- `backend()` --calls--> `LocalBackend`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_memory_system.py → headroom/memory/backends/local.py
- `test_classify_client_recognises_known_harness_user_agents()` --calls--> `classify_client()`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_request_outcome.py → headroom/proxy/auth_mode.py
- `test_classify_client_x_client_header_wins_over_user_agent()` --calls--> `classify_client()`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_request_outcome.py → headroom/proxy/auth_mode.py
- `fresh_store()` --calls--> `reset_compression_store()`  [INFERRED]
  tests/test_ccr_mcp_server.py → headroom/cache/compression_store.py

## Hyperedges (group relationships)
- **proxy_telemetry_v2 schema evolution: create → add cache_bust_tokens → add stack/install_mode** — sql_proxy_telemetry_v2, sql_upgrade_telemetry_cache_bust, sql_upgrade_telemetry_stack_context, db_table_proxy_telemetry_v2 [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **dashboard_summary schema evolution: create → add hourly_stats → drop cache_bust_stats** — sql_dashboard_summary, sql_upgrade_dashboard_v2, sql_upgrade_telemetry_cache_bust, db_table_dashboard_summary, fn_refresh_dashboard_summary [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **Rust workspace: headroom-core + headroom-proxy + headroom-py + headroom-parity** — rust_crate_headroom_core, rust_crate_headroom_proxy, rust_crate_headroom_py, rust_crate_headroom_parity [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **Rust signals module: Tiered<T> combinator over KeywordDetector implementing LineImportanceDetector** — signals_tiered_combinator, signals_keyword_detector, signals_line_importance_detector, rust_crate_headroom_core [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **Docker memory stack: headroom-proxy + qdrant (vector DB) + neo4j (graph DB)** — docker_image_headroom, docker_service_qdrant, docker_service_neo4j, docker_compose_yml [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **Windows install flow: install.ps1 → pulls Docker image → writes headroom.ps1 + headroom.cmd → adds to PATH** — install_ps1_script, docker_image_headroom, wrapper_headroom_ps1 [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **9-Phase Realignment Plan (40 PRs, ~13 weeks sequential / ~8 weeks parallel)** — phase_a_lockdown, phase_b_live_zone, phase_c_rust_proxy, phase_d_bedrock_vertex, phase_e_cache_stabilization, phase_f_auth_mode, phase_g_rtk_observability, phase_h_python_retirement, phase_i_test_infra [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **Type-Aware Compressor Suite (all kept)** — smart_crusher, log_compressor, diff_compressor, search_compressor, kompress_compressor [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **Auth Mode Policy Matrix (PAYG/OAuth/Subscription gates compression behavior)** — auth_mode_payg, auth_mode_oauth, auth_mode_subscription, auth_mode_classifier [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **Differential Network Capture (3-lane mitmproxy for direct vs headroom comparison)** — docker_service_mitm_direct, docker_service_mitm_headroom_client, docker_service_mitm_headroom_upstream, docker_service_headroom_proxy_diff, docker_service_claude_direct, docker_service_claude_headroom [EXTRACTED 1.00]
- **Headroom Plugin System (oauth2, openclaw, agent-hooks)** — plugin_headroom_oauth2, plugin_openclaw, plugin_headroom_agent_hooks [EXTRACTED 1.00]
